We are a society of people with wide mindsets, all primarily interested in Mathematics who actively plan to organize different academic and cultural events. Greetings from MathSoc! 

Remember the days when you spent hours on getting those funky integrals right? We are here to recreate that experience, together with a competitive environment! 

MathSoc invites all mathletes in IIT Delhi to an evening full of integrals, Integration Bee 2022.
It is a contest where you get the chance to compete with your fellow mathletes to solve involving problems curated by us. 

The event will feature two rounds:
1. Preliminary Round- A set of 20 questions will be given to the participants in a time bound manner. The TOP 16 solvers will proceed to the finals. Duration: 30 mins 
2. Finals- The TOP 16 will compete in a knockout championship, solving integrals side by side with chalk on board! 

Time: 3:00 P.M, 12th October 2022
Venue: LH325
Participation: Individual
Registration: Walk-In 
Walk-ins are allowed but weâ€™d appreciate if you filled out this small form for us.

b)exothermic reaction

3.This was a question on CFT .Basically i guess it was on draw the structure and predict the spin

4.This was a standard jee question which we used to do.You are given an unknown amount of NaHCO3 and Na2Co3.You are asked to find their specific amount.For this titration is carried out one with phenolphthalein which is continued by methyl orange.

5.This was a question on acetylferrocene.As you know if we use anhydrous Alcl3 we get disubstituted product.Moreover we were asked to compare the Rf values.

6.This was a question on the mechanism of preparation of the compound in exp6(i guess i cannot recall the name of the compound ,the nitrogen based benzene ring one)

7.This was a question on the first experiment .I think they asked if en could replace bipyridyl  and why is muerixide used as an indicator?

8.This was a question on the quantum mechanical treatment.They asked to change the equation parameters and find a solution which has j as a parameter instead of n where j is the number of double bond and n is the number of atoms

9.This was a question on carotene.I guess you could check up atkins .There is a solved example there where they have asked about the length of the chain and for this we need to consider excitation from HUMO to LUMO

10.Here they asked about the conductometric curves for various pair of solutions.
WA SB , WB SA, SA SB, Two salts ,WA SA SB.. and so on.

There was just one more question which i am unable to recall.
There were total of 11 questions ,each question carried a weightage of approx 4 marks.
And yes you need to remember a bit of jee stuff ,only manual wont suffice.

12/22/22, 10:59 - +91 95820 98771: The IIT Kanpur Stamatics society is hosting an online mathematics competition, Mathemania, on the 26th and 27th of December. Mathemania is an open competition designed to bring together bright students from various institutes and allow them to showcase their mathematical abilities. There are no pre-requisites to register and the questions do not require advanced math knowledge.
The competition is a team event varying from one to four members. There are three rounds, the first two being elimination rounds on the 26th, followed by a final round on 27th. There will be an online portal where the question paper will be uploaded, and every team will have a set amount of time to submit their work and answers. The theme for Mathemania 2022 is the Hunger Games! 
Register using the link below and have loads of fun ! 
May the best tribute win!
The deadline for registration is 25th December, 11:59 pm.
The registration link: https://forms.gle/PMMkSz6SAmmm5Pw99
Join our discord server for further updates and announcements : https://discord.gg/PFKtMeFW
Please contact the coordinators for any further questions.

Thank you in advance.

Greetings from *NSS IIT Delhi!*
NSS IIT Delhi is going to organize Rengreza a flagship event of *Kaizen* 2023. *Rangreza* is about sustainable and green fashion. It is a fashion show competition with each team comprising of *4 to 6 participants* each of who all are going to present their ideas towards green fashion.

A green fashion show typically refers to a fashion event that showcases clothing and accessories made from sustainable and eco-friendly materials, as well as designs that promote environmental and social responsibility. The aim of such a show is to raise awareness about the impact of the fashion industry on the environment and to promote sustainable fashion practices.
